            "description": "Orange3-bioinformatics\n=======================\n\n<a href=\"https://dev.azure.com/orange-biolab/orange3-bioinformatics/\">\n  <img src=\"https://dev.azure.com/orange-biolab/orange3-bioinformatics/_apis/build/status/biolab.orange3-bioinformatics?branchName=master\" />\n</a>\n\n<a href='https://orange3-bioinformatics.readthedocs.io/en/latest/?badge=latest'>\n    <img src='https://readthedocs.org/projects/orange3-bioinformatics/badge/?version=latest' alt='Documentation Status' />\n</a>\n\n<a href=\"https://codecov.io/gh/biolab/orange3-bioinformatics\">\n  <img src=\"https://codecov.io/gh/biolab/orange3-bioinformatics/branch/master/graph/badge.svg\" />\n</a>\n\n<a href=\"https://pypi.org/project/Orange3-Bioinformatics/\">\n  <img alt=\"PyPI\" src=\"https://img.shields.io/pypi/v/orange3-bioinformatics.svg\" />\n</a>\n\n<a href=\"https://anaconda.org/conda-forge/orange3-bioinformatics\">\n  <img alt=\"Conda\" src=\"https://img.shields.io/conda/v/conda-forge/orange3-bioinformatics.svg\" />\n</a>\n\n<a href=\"https://pypi.org/project/Orange3-Bioinformatics/\">\n  <img alt=\"PyPI - License\" src=\"https://img.shields.io/pypi/l/orange3-bioinformatics.svg\" />\n</a>\n\n\nOrange Bioinformatics extends Orange, a data mining software\npackage, with common functionality for bioinformatics. The provided\nfunctionality can be accessed as a Python library or through a visual\nprogramming interface (Orange Canvas). The latter is also suitable for\nnon-programmers.\n\nIn Orange Canvas the analyst connects basic computational units, called\nwidgets, into data flow analytics schemas. Two units-widgets can be\nconnected if they share a data type. Compared to other popular tools like\nTaverna, Orange widgets are high-level, integrated potentially complex\ntasks, but are specific enough to be used independently. Even elaborate\nanalyses rarely consist of more than ten widgets; while tasks such as\nclustering and enrichment analysis could be executed with up to five\nwidgets. While building the schema each widget is independently controlled\nwith settings, the settings do not conceptually burden the analyst.\n\nOrange Bioinformatics provides access to publicly available data, like GEO data sets, GO and KEGG.\nAll features can be combined with powerful visualization, network exploration and\ndata mining techniques from the Orange data mining framework.\n\nInstallation\n------------\n\nTo install the add-on with pip use\n\n    pip install Orange3-bioinformatics\n\nTo register this add-on with Orange, but keep the code in the development directory (do not copy it to\nPython's site-packages directory), run\n\n    pip install -e .\n\nDocumentation / widget help can be built by running\n\n    make html htmlhelp\n\nfrom the doc directory.\n\nUsage\n-----\n\nAfter the installation, the widgets from this add-on are registered with Orange. To run Orange from the terminal, use\n\n    python3 -m Orange.canvas\n\nor\n\n    orange-canvas\n\nThe new widgets are in the toolbox bar under Bioinformatics section.\n\n\n",

            "description": "Textable\n========\n\nTextable is an open source add-on bringing advanced text-analytical\nfunctionalities to the `Orange Canvas <http://orange.biolab.si/>`_ data mining\nsoftware package (itself open source). Look at the following `example\n<http://orange-textable.readthedocs.io/en/latest/illustration.html>`_ to see\nit in typical action.\n\nThe project's website is http://textable.io. It hosts a repository of\n`recipes <http://textable.io/find-recipes>`_ to help you get started with\nTextable.\n\nDocumentation is hosted at http://orange3-textable.readthedocs.io/ and\nyou can get further support at https://textable.freshdesk.com/ or by e-mail\nto `support@textable.io <mailto:support@textable.io>`_\n\nOrange Textable was designed and implemented by `LangTech Sarl\n<http://langtech.ch>`_ on behalf of the `department of language and\ninformation sciences (SLI) <http://www.unil.ch/sli>`_ at the `University of\nLausanne <http://www.unil.ch>`_ (see `Credits\n<http://orange-textable.readthedocs.io/en/latest/credits.html>`_ and\n`How to cite Orange Textable\n<http://orange-textable.readthedocs.io/en/latest/citing.html>`_).\n\nFeatures\n--------\n\nBasic text analysis\n~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~\n\n* use regular expressions to segment letters, words, sentences, etc. or full-text query\n* use regexes to extract annotations from many input formats\n* import in-line XML markup (e.g. TEI)\n* include/exclude segments based on user-defined lists (stoplists)\n* filter segments based on frequency\n* easily generate random text samples\n\nAdvanced text analysis\n~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~\n\n* concordances and collocations, also based on annotations\n* segment distribution, document-term matrix, transition matrix, etc.\n* co-occurrence tables, also between different types of segments\n* lemmatization and POS-tagging via Treetagger\n* robust linguistic complexity measures, incl. mean length of word, lexical diversity, etc.\n* many advanced data mining algorithms: clustering, classification, factor analyses, etc.\n\nText recoding\n~~~~~~~~~~~~~\n\n* Unicode-aware preprocessing functions, e.g. remove accents from Ancient Greek text\n* recode and restructure texts using regexes, e.g. rewrite CSV as XML\n\nExtensibility\n~~~~~~~~~~~~~\n\n* handles hundreds of text files\n* use Python script for custom text processing or to access external tools: NLTK, Pattern, GenSim, etc.\n\nInteroperability\n~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~\n\n* import text from keyboard, files, or URLs\n* process any kind of raw text format: TXT, HTML, XML, CSV, etc.\n* supports many text encodings, incl. Unicode\n* export results in text files or copy-paste\n* easy interfacing with Orange's Text Mining add-on\n\nEase of access\n~~~~~~~~~~~~~~\n\n* user-friendly visual interface\n* ready-made recipes for a range of frequent use cases\n* extensive documentation\n* support and community forums\n\n\n",
